                                    <h5>About the Book</h5>
                                </div>
                                <div id="ProductInfoTabContent" class="content accordion-tab-content active more-block">
                                    <div id="book_more" class="book_more">
                                        <DIV><P>In this exciting Level 1 Green Light Reader Gossie, Gertie, BooBoo, and Peedie are all dyeing Easter eggs. Ollie wants Easter eggs too and he has a plan for how to get them! Dunrea again gets the preschooler emotions exactly right, capturing a range of holiday-inspired feelings, from Ollie&#39;s wiggly impatience to be included to the pure joy of the older goslings discovering that Ollie has arranged the best Easter egg hunt of all.</P></DIV>
                                    </div>

                                <div class="title accordion-tab-title AboutTheAuthorTab AboutTheAuthor-accordion show-for-small" data-hash="AboutTheAuthor-accordion" data-parent-tab-content="AboutTheAuthorTab" data-parent-tab="tabAboutTheAuthor">
                                    <h5>About the Author</h5>
                                </div>
                                <div id="AboutTheAuthorTabContent" class="content accordion-tab-content more-block">
                                    
                                            <section class="row featured-content nine-column blurb">
                                                <div class="three columns image-wrap">
                                                    <figure class="image-wrap">
                                                        <img id="_2310708db40f3f_authorRepeater_authorImageUrl_0" class="itemImage" src="/shop/books/assets/contributor/dunrea$olivier.gif" />
                                                    </figure>
                                                </div>
                                                <div class="nine columns text-box">
                                                    <h2>
                                                        Olivier Dunrea</h2>
                                                    <p>
                                                        Olivier Dunrea is the creator of beautiful and well-loved children&rsquo;s books. A painter and a sculptor, his work centers around farms, animals, architecture, and folklore. He lives in the tiny village of Narrowsburg, New York, in the Catskill Mountains.
                                                        <!--<a id="_2310708db40f3f_authorRepeater_authorReadMoreHyperlink_0" class="arrow" href="/bookstore/authors/Olivier-Dunrea/569704">Read More</a>-->
                                                    </p>
                                                </div>

                            <li id="ReviewsTab" class="accordion-tab">

                                    <h5>Reviews</h5>
                                </div>
                                <div id="ReviewsTabContent" class="content accordion-tab-content more-block">
                                    <div id="reviewsDiv">
                                        <div id="reviews_more" class="reviews_more">
                                            <DIV><P>"The simple declarative phrases and gently humorous illustrations are just right for the age group...Stickers are included."--<I>Publishers Weekly</I></P><P>"Gossie and her friends are back, dyeing Easter eggs...As in the other "Gossie and Friends" books, the illustrations are bright watercolors against a white background. Fans and newcomers alike will be delighted with this latest installment."--<I>School Library Journal</I></P><P>"As with all of his books, the overall effect is just this side of too-cute-for-words, landing it in exactly the right range of adorable. Although toddlers and young preschoolers may be mystified at the madness behind Ollie&#8217;s method, as he steals his compatriots&#8217; hidden eggs and then hides them again, there&#8217;ll be more than pleased by his triumphant ending."--<I>Kirkus</I></P></DIV>

<script type="text/javascript">

    $(document).ready(function () {
        var newCookieVal;
        $(document.body).on('click touchstart', '.cookie-val', function () {
            var currentCookieVal = $(this).attr('data-cookie-val');
            var cookieName = 'cookiepersona';
            var cookiedomain = '.hmhco.com';
            newCookieVal = currentCookieVal;
            document.cookie = cookieName + "=" + newCookieVal + ";domain=" + cookiedomain + ";path=/";
            // alert(document.cookie + " new cookie value");
        });
       
    });

</script>

<script>

    equalheight = function (container) {

        var currentTallest = 0,
             currentRowStart = 0,
             rowDivs = new Array(),
             $el,
             topPosition = 0;
        $(container).each(function () {

            $el = $(this);
            $($el).height('auto')
            topPostion = $el.position().top;

            if (currentRowStart != topPostion) {
                for (currentDiv = 0 ; currentDiv < rowDivs.length ; currentDiv++) {
                    rowDivs[currentDiv].height(currentTallest);
                }
                rowDivs.length = 0; // empty the array
                currentRowStart = topPostion;
                currentTallest = $el.height();
                rowDivs.push($el);
            } else {
                rowDivs.push($el);
                currentTallest = (currentTallest < $el.height()) ? ($el.height()) : (currentTallest);
            }
            for (currentDiv = 0 ; currentDiv < rowDivs.length ; currentDiv++) {
                rowDivs[currentDiv].height(currentTallest);
            }
        });
    }
    $(window).load(function () {
        if ($('.fixed-grid').length >= 0) {
            equalheight('.fixed-grid.block-grid.one-up.featured-content li section');
            equalheight('.fixed-grid.block-grid.two-up.featured-content li section .nine.columns .heading-wrap');
            equalheight('.fixed-grid.block-grid.two-up.featured-content li section');
            equalheight('.fixed-grid.block-grid.three-up.featured-content li section .nine.columns .heading-wrap');
            equalheight('.fixed-grid.block-grid.four-up.featured-content li section .nine.columns .heading-wrap');
            equalheight('.fixed-grid.block-grid.three-up.featured-content li section');
            equalheight('.fixed-grid.block-grid.four-up.featured-content li section');
            equalheight('.fixed-grid.block-grid.three-up.account-types li section');
        }
        if ($('.fluid-grid').length <= 0) {
            equalheight('.row.featured-content.nine-column.four-items.widget-section .content-wrap.twelve.columns .text-wrap');
            equalheight('.row.featured-content.nine-column.two-items.widget-section.eventext .six.columns');
            equalheight('.row.featured-content.nine-column.two-items.widget-section.eventext .six.columns .content-wrap.twelve.columns .text-wrap');
        }
        if ($('.bkgdLightGray').length >= 0) {
            equalheight('.bkgdLightGray .padding10');
            resizeA();
            equalheight('.bkgdLightGray .padding10 h6');
            equalheight('.bkgdLightGray .padding10 p:not(".cta")');
        }
        if ($('.eachAddressCol').length >= 0) {
            equalheight('.eachAddressCol');
        }
        if ($(window).width() < 641) {
            equalheight('.fluid-grid.block-grid.two-up.featured-content li section');
        }
    });
    /*if ($('.bkgdLightGray').length >= 0) {
        $('.bkgdLightGray .padding10 img').on('load', function () {
            alert($(this).height());
        });
    }*/
    $(window).resize(function () {
        equalheight('.bkgdLightGray .padding10');
        equalheight('.bkgdLightGray .padding10 h6');
        resizeA();
        equalheight('.bkgdLightGray .padding10 p:not(".cta")');
        equalheight('.fixed-grid.block-grid.one-up.featured-content li section');
        equalheight('.fixed-grid.block-grid.two-up.featured-content li section .nine.columns .heading-wrap');
        equalheight('.fixed-grid.block-grid.two-up.featured-content li section');
        equalheight('.fixed-grid.block-grid.three-up.featured-content li section .nine.columns .heading-wrap');
        equalheight('.fixed-grid.block-grid.four-up.featured-content li section .nine.columns .heading-wrap');
        equalheight('.fixed-grid.block-grid.three-up.featured-content li section');
        equalheight('.fixed-grid.block-grid.four-up.featured-content li section');
        equalheight('.row.featured-content.nine-column.four-items.widget-section .content-wrap.twelve.columns .text-wrap');
        equalheight('.row.featured-content.nine-column.two-items.widget-section.eventext .six.columns');
        equalheight('.row.featured-content.nine-column.two-items.widget-section.eventext .six.columns .content-wrap.twelve.columns .text-wrap');
        if ($(window).width() < 641) {
            equalheight('.fluid-grid.block-grid.two-up.featured-content li section');
        }
    });
    $(document).ready(function () {
        resizeA();
    });
    function resizeA() {
        if ($('.bkgdLightGray').length >= 0) {
            var maxHeight = -1;

            $('.bkgdLightGray .padding10 a img').each(function () {
                maxHeight = maxHeight > $(this).height() ? maxHeight : $(this).height();
            });

            $('.bkgdLightGray .padding10 a:first-child:not(".button")').each(function () {
                $(this).height(maxHeight);
            });
        }
    }
</script>

            $(document).ready(function () {
                $('.modal').click(function (e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    var urlValue = $(this).data('href');
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        $('#modal #modal_content').load(urlValue); // Load its linked page into the div
                        $("#modal").reveal({
                            closeOnBackgroundClick: true,
                            dismissModalClass: 'close-reveal-modal'
                        });
                    }, 500);
                });
                $('.close-reveal-modal').click(function () {
                    $("#modal").trigger("reveal:close");

        function Om_AddProductToCart(title, currentCartCount, quantity, productCode, isProductDetail) {
            var oAdd = GetOmObj();

            if (currentCartCount == 1) {
                oAdd.events = "scAdd,scOpen";
                oAdd.linkTrackEvents = "scAdd,scOpen";
            }
            else {
                oAdd.events = "scAdd";
                oAdd.linkTrackEvents = "scAdd";
            }

            oAdd.pageName = dl.pageName;
            oAdd.eVar1 = '';
            oAdd.products = ';' + productCode + ':' + title;
            oAdd.hier1 = dl.hier1;

            oAdd.linkTrackVars += ",products,eVar1,hier1,events";
            oAdd.tl(true, 'o', 'Add to Cart');

            if (DEBUG_CLICK)
                alert('Add to Cart complete');
        }

        function Om_CartFunction(action, isbn) {
            var oCart = GetOmObj();

            oCart.prop19 = action;
            oCart.linkTrackVars += ",prop19,products";

            //By default, we need to set the ISBN here. It may get overridden at a later place
            if (isbn != '')
                oCart.products = ';' + isbn;

            if (action == 'checkout') {
                oCart.events = 'scCheckout';
                oCart.linkTrackEvents = 'scCheckout';

                for (var i = 0; i < currentCartItems.length; i++) {
                    if (i == 0) {
                        oCart.products = ";" + currentCartItems[i];
                    }
                    else {
                        oCart.products += ",;" + currentCartItems[i];
                    }
                }
            }
            else if (action == 'remove') {
                oCart.events = 'scRemove';
                oCart.linkTrackEvents = 'scRemove';
            }
            else if (action == 'viewcart') {
                oCart.events = 'scView';
                oCart.linkTrackEvents = 'scView';
            }

            oCart.tl(true, 'o', 'Cart Function: ' + action);

            if (DEBUG_CLICK)
                alert('Cart Function Click (' + action + ') complete');
        }

        // a is the a tag clicked
        function trackImgClick($a, parent) {
            parent = parent || $a.parent();
            try {
                // get <a>'s inner img's src
                var filename = ($a.find('img').attr('src') || '')
                    // get last token of /
                    .split('/').pop()
                    // get first token of ?
                    .split('?').shift();
                var banner = parent;
                // only filename required, banner name is not
                var result = filename;
                console.log(result);
                // omniture
                Om_ImgClick(result);

            } catch (ex) {
                console.error(ex);
            }
        }

        //tracking succesful registration - gomath registration
        function Om_RegisterClick(email) {
            var oRegister = GetOmObj();
            oRegister.eVar2 = "GMA";
            oRegister.eVar6 = email;
            oRegister.events = "event9,event3";

        function Om_ItemClick(item) {
            var oItemClick = GetOmObj();
            var itemAttr = item.attr('data-section');
            var itemText = item.text();

            if (itemAttr == 't.t2') //category
            {
                itemText = itemText.substring(0, itemText.indexOf('(') - 1);
                oItemClick.prop49 = itemText;
            }
            if (itemAttr == 't.t3') //sub-category
            {
                itemText = itemText.substring(0, itemText.indexOf('(') - 1);
                oItemClick.prop50 = itemText;
            }
            else if (itemAttr == 'topic') {
                itemText = itemText.substring(0, itemText.indexOf('(') - 1);
                oItemClick.prop51 = itemText;
            }

            if (itemAttr == 'paging') {
                oItemClick.pageName = 'Search Results:' + item.text();
                //oItemClick.linkTrackVars += ",pageName";
                //oItemClick.tl(true, 'o', 'PageName: ' + item.text());
            }
            else if (itemAttr == 'pagingprev' || itemAttr == 'pagingnext') {
                itemSearch = item[0].search;
                var items = itemSearch.split(';');
                var pageNumber = '';
                var hasPageNumber = false;
                for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                    var kvp = items[i].split('=');
                    if (kvp[0] == "page") {
                        pageNumber = kvp[1];
                        hasPageNumber = true;
                        break;
                    }
                }
                if (hasPageNumber == false)
                    pageNumber = 1;

                oItemClick.pageName = ' Search Results:' + pageNumber;
                oItemClick.linkTrackVars += ",pageName";
                oItemClick.tl(true, 'o', 'PageName: ' + pageNumber);
            }

            if (DEBUG_CLICK) {
                alert('Item Click: ' + item.text());
            }
        }

            //Analytics Variables which replaces omniture/ComponentBrowse
            dl.contentcategory = 'Browse';

            //Derived fields
            dl.membershiptypepathing = dl.membershiptype + ':' + dl.pageName;
            dl.programhpvideoplay = gradeSelect;
            dl.paymenttype = stateSelect;
            dl.programhpshopnow = sortSelect;

            if (DEBUG_CLICK)
                alert('Category Browse complete');
        }

        // Omniture tracking script for Carousel Image tracking
        function carouselTracking(imgName) {

            var oCarousel = GetOmObj();
            oCarousel.linkTrackVars = "eVar40,events";
            oCarousel.linkTrackEvents = "event43";
            oCarousel.events = "event43";
            oCarousel.eVar40 = imgName;
            oCarousel.tl(true, 'o', 'Carousel tracking');
        }

        // Omniture tracking script for Callout Image tracking
        function calloutTracking(imgName) {
            var oCallout = GetOmObj();
            oCallout.linkTrackVars = "prop58";
            oCallout.prop58 = imgName;
            oCallout.tl(true, 'o', 'Sub-Box Tracking');
        }

    // tracks read more/less
    function Om_ReadMoreOrLess(newLink) {
        var oLink = GetOmObj();
        isbn13Val = '9780544809116';
        if (newLink == "moreLink") {
            oLink.prop10 = isbn13Val;
            oLink.linkTrackVars += ",prop10";
        }
        else {
            oLink.prop9 = isbn13Val;
            oLink.linkTrackVars += ",prop9";
        }

        oLink.tl(true, 'o', newLink);

        // debug
        if (DEBUG_CLICK) {
            alert(newLink);
        }
    }
